Mr. Moon Sun-myung's Words Compilation Committee

                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
I Didn't Realize
<Prayer> This month marks the third Sabbath. Please remember your young children gathered here this morning. 
No matter how different each person's circumstances and positions may be, our hearts longing for you must unite as one. As we think of the fact that we are connected through you, may we become children who can hold onto that bond and rejoice and grieve, even in any living environment, in the path of suffering, or in sorrowful places, inheriting the inseparable bond of blood. 
We have come to know in a true sense that you are our Father, but as we reflect on what you are observing, whom you are visiting, and whom you are encouraging at this time, we realize that there is no one on this earth who understands your will. It is indeed true that there is no group of people on this earth pursuing your heart. Only we, the inadequate ones, know that you are present and what your circumstances are. 
Father, there are many proud nations and many proud people in the world, but since such nations and people are in a position where they cannot connect with you, you must inevitably turn to us, even if we are not the sons and daughters you wish to find, and with hope and expectation, you must send us as messengers to the place where you can find the sons and daughters you desire. We understand that this is your position. 
Father, it is exceedingly difficult for us, the inadequate ones, to bear the tremendous mission you have to find individuals, families, nations, and the world through those who serve as messengers. Knowing this, it is indeed a miserable and sorrowful fact that you must worry about us and be concerned for us. 
Father, whenever we bow before you, may we be allowed to truly look up to you with reverence as we present ourselves before you. We must become people who know that you are our Father, who have pioneered the path of suffering behind history, unknown to anyone. Even if we are disabled, we must have the firm heart that says, "I am connected to my Father and Son. Nothing can sever this bond." 
When a parent with a disabled child is in a position to establish their authority and dignity, they can uphold their dignity when they have sons and daughters who are better and superior to their enemies. However, when they call the disabled children their sons and daughters and ask their enemies to repay them, they cannot help but think of how much their enemies will mock and ridicule them. 
We know that we have disgraced you in such positions on the path of restoration. My appearance, my gait, my actions, and my life have all been a source of shame before you. From that standpoint, if there is a way to fly away, I would want to fly away, and if there is a place to disappear, I would want to disappear. Was that not your heart? Yet, you, who have only disabled children, cannot help but hold onto them and cannot help but hope that through these sons and daughters, you will leave behind descendants who will be greater than the children of your enemies. 
Even though we, the disabled children, have become a source of insult to you, thinking of the fact that we have instead become a group of betrayers and rebels against you, we cannot help but discover that we, who are your descendants, are ashamed to call you our Father. 
Father, we, such as we are, have come before you again at this time, so if mercy is your essence and compassion is your nature, please forgive us once more. Knowing our historical mistakes, we pledge never to become such again, and if you stand in a shameful position because of us, we must become sons and daughters who feel the mission to restore your dignity, even if it means being shamed a million times. No matter how many times we die, we must think that this is the only path we can take to overturn the environment of shame where our enemies mock us and to push aside the position where they boast of their children. 
Even if the children of our enemies betray one another and go down the path of unfilial conduct towards their parents, we must be better in our filial piety. Even as disabled children, if we dedicate our lives joyfully for you, we know there is a way to boast in heaven and earth. Since there is only that one path, we must understand the internal situation of our Father, who could not help but say, "Those who wish to die will live, and those who wish to live will die." 
Father, we must not become a pitiful group that engages in habitual faith life and presents a habitual appearance before you. We must become sons and daughters who are appropriate in your heart. Not only must we be remembered in your heart, but we must also become sons and daughters who can stand in the position of serving the Father, who tirelessly works day and night to lay the foundation for victory over our enemies. We know how difficult it is to stand in that position. We understand that it is truly difficult for inadequate children to stand in the position of serving you because there is only one path. 
However, Father, we must strive to reach such a position. We must struggle, even if it means writhing in agony. We must have the appearance of advancing and advancing toward that place, crying out day and night. Even if we are disabled, we must go forward, even if it means crawling, and if we cannot do that, we must go for you, even if it means crawling on our bellies. We must not forget that this is our situation and position. 
Father, we have come to know that there are no other pitiful beings on this earth besides us. Because we are pitiful on this earth, we must also understand that you, who treat us, are pitiful. We must truly understand this. Father, how terrible, how shameful, and how humiliating it is for us to stand before you while the arduous path of restoration still remains to guide us. Therefore, if you do not appear to us and at least promise us, we must have the mindset of striving to walk this path, and we must strive to avoid putting you in a position of shame because of our enemies. 
Today, we, who have come before you this morning, entrust our bodies and hearts to you once again. We are like beggars in tattered clothes, and we have come before you in a shameful and disabled state. However, our hearts are determined to fulfill the duties of filial piety and to uphold the principles of loyalty, so we earnestly hope and wish that you will be with us at this time. 
Father, please remember your children scattered across the nation. Moreover, we know that the church leaders who are training and have reached their posts are worshiping before you this morning with the same heart, so please hold their hearts and guide their paths. May they become those who know that nothing can be done without you, and may they fulfill their responsibilities and become the heavenly filial sons and daughters who comfort you. 
Father, please hold onto the mobilization members scattered around the world. They are a pitiful group, appearing on this earth for the first time under the name of the "Crusaders of Peace." If they are pitiful, they are indeed a pitiful group, and if they are lonely, they are a lonely group. Since you have raised them in the world, please allow them to walk straight, even if they shed blood, sweat, and tears. And may you allow your presence to be revealed wherever they go and wherever they stay. 
When your children cannot carry out this purpose, they become pitiful beings, and your path becomes a path of despair. Therefore, please protect this final path and love this group. We earnestly hope that this will become a historic opportunity to resolve your historical shame and a memorial for us, so please be with them and mobilize the heavenly hosts to encourage them. May they become the warriors without shame who must bear the mission of restoration, holding the earth in your embrace, and may you remember those who stand on the front lines. 
Now, August 20 has passed. After August, September will come. At this time, having passed more than half of this year, we must reflect on the past and think about the many issues we must settle before you. Since we cannot find the conditions for resolving those issues while considering ourselves, may we become a group that offers ourselves completely, saying, "Even if we are unfilial, we are your sons, so do as you will." We earnestly hope that you will allow 1972 to become a historic year in establishing your nation. 
We earnestly hope that 1972 will become a year of memories, reflections, and praises that will shine brightly in your nation, your world, and your history. 
Now, please take Korea into your hands. Father, who has come to this pitiful nation, if you cannot bind the future of this nation into one in your hands, will you not become an even more pitiful Father? We, the unworthy ones, are divided in heart and body centered around one individual. Men and women are divided, families are divided, tribes, nations, and the world are divided, heaven and earth are divided, and people and God are divided. Who will build the bridge between them? 
We know that it is necessary to unite you and me into one family, like an impregnable fortress where individuals cannot separate from each other, but who will fulfill that mission? Fallen humanity cannot do it. 
That is why we are hoping for the cooperation of the countless saints in the spirit world. Before you bind this together and unify it, there is no way to be united. Our strength, standing in the same fate as those being swept away by the flood, is utterly insufficient, so please look upon us with pity, as we call you Father and call upon our ancestors. 
When you ask where there is a family that you can visit, we know there is none. In order to find such a path and such a family, the Unification Church has established families with new meanings. This is because we know that no nation or people can go before you without you going first. You must know that the establishment of different families was because you demanded a unified path. 
Is it not to make what was two into one and possess it as your own? 
We have gathered these families to form tribes. Among those tribes, we know there are Abel tribes and Cain tribes. The Abel tribes cannot inherit the ideal realm of the parents or the ideal world of God's love without restoring the Cain tribes, and that is the principle. Therefore, we are striving with all our strength, struggling and writhing, rushing toward the tribal realm that can restore Cain, so please remember this group of unification. Remember the blessed families. 
After forming a united tribe, we must take that and form a nation, and we have the responsibility to unite the Abel nation with the Cain nation. Therefore, we know that our desire is to achieve the independence of this nation, the unification of this nation, and the second liberation of this nation. Father, you must take charge of the future of Korea. No one can be the owner, so we earnestly hope that you will be with us. 
Since you are certainly alive, we believe and know that you will fulfill your purpose, so we earnestly hope that you will stand with this pitiful group and fulfill your will. 
We must unify Korea and gather the three nations of Asia, namely the Adam nation, the Hae-wha nation, and the Archangel nation. The center must be you. We do not wish for this for the glory of any individual, but for the historical glory, the glory of the times, the glory of our descendants, and for the glory of the Father who has labored. Please remember this pitiful group. 
Until now, we have walked this path. Today, we must continue on this path and run toward that battlefield. Tomorrow, we must walk that path. We must gaze at the enemy's stronghold and endure, endure, and endure, tirelessly fulfilling the duties of filial piety and loyalty. Not only must you praise us as the essence of filial piety and loyalty, but also, before all the hosts of heaven and all people, and before the countless saints of the historical age, may you stand us up and say, "These are my beloved ones, my life among lives, my hope among hopes."
I will make sure that you can inherit your eternal victory's achievements. I know that it is your wish to see such children appear on this earth. Therefore, we must strive towards that direction and run towards it, even if only in our hearts.

Father, you have led the unfortunate Korean people, who have suffered through the path of indemnity for a long time, to this point. There is no one but you who can guide this nation in the future. We know that when we worship you, we prosper. We also know that when you are with us, that nation will thrive, so please do not abandon the unfortunate multitude, and you must be with us. When you are with us, this nation will become a great nation in Asia that no other people can follow.

It is not a matter of hope but a matter of action; it is not a matter of words but a matter of practice. If the sons and daughters who are sprinting towards this path are here this morning, please bless them. I earnestly ask that you grant the deep yearning of our hearts and allow us to be inevitable children who can embrace your heart and inspire you more than anyone else.

Please remember once again your children scattered throughout South Korea, and remember those who are fighting in the lonely path throughout the ages. Please remember the workers of unification who are struggling under the enemy's world, fighting for their lives. When their limits of toil are reached, please trample upon the authority of Satan that is moving the world on this earth, so that they may greet the day of glory, the day of liberation, and the new morning of brightness with praise. May the connections of the unification world spread and bloom flowers on the hearts of individuals, and may the path of unification be opened so that we can raise the banner of freedom and life in the dark world. This path is not for people but for you, so I earnestly ask that you allow your glory to arise here.

Now, as we bow before you, Father, embracing you in a bond that cannot be severed, if you could make this holy morning a time to receive the command of tomorrow's duty and mission, I would have no further wishes. Please do not leave us alone and come to us again.

May everything be fulfilled within the will you have granted, and may this morning be one that you can remember with joy. I pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Words> We know that there are not many people among humanity living on this earth who understand from what starting point of history they have come, what process they have gone through, and to what purpose they are heading.

Setting that aside, even among the many religious people, especially those who seek God and regard Him as their parent, centered around Christianity, we know that there are not many who clearly understand how they have started, what process they have gone through, and what destination they will reach.

How will God relate to us?

Furthermore, beyond such humanity, there are special individuals who are earnestly engaging in spiritual experiences, or mystical experiences, or living while personally feeling the transcendent world. In other words, those who are spiritually connected or those who stand at the highest position in the true sense of the moral standard—do they know where they started, what process they have gone through, and where they are headed in relation to the spiritual world? They do not know for sure. While they may receive instructions or guidance from the spiritual realm, no one knows the issue of where it started, what content it involves, and what relationship it is establishing through their current selves.

Looking at Paul or Peter in the early Christian era, we can see that they based their faith on God as the essence of their lives, as we can understand through the scriptures. However, we can also glimpse the fact that they struggled and moved forward without clearly knowing the fundamental origin of why such events occurred and what process they would take to establish a relationship with the reality of this world.

The early church was able to perform actions that could transcend persecution due to spiritual history, but it remained limited in scope, unable to expand from individuals to nations and globally. This was because they could not clearly grasp the fundamental cause of how such spiritual phenomena affected them and what direction they were heading towards through what process. Therefore, we must recognize that the spiritual history that existed in the early church was interrupted along the way.

Today, Christian theologians often regard those who engage in spiritual history as individuals doing evil. They believe that seeking that path is dangerous, and since it leads to results where one cannot hope for a normal purpose, modern theology has become one that cannot even acknowledge it. When we think about those who learn such theology and lead the church, we must consider that they stand in a position where such matters are not their concern.

So, how will God relate to us? This is the issue. Of course, it is through truth that we establish a relationship, but at that time, we must speak. Although we are strangers to each other, we share our circumstances through words. Here, "circumstances" do not refer to the current situation. With such circumstances, we cannot establish a deep connection. The longer those circumstances have existed, the more we can share them with friends, and the more difficult those circumstances are, the more we can share them with friends, creating a space where we can empathize with those difficulties, thus forming true friendships. In such a space, true connections can also be established.

The greater the internal connection that allows us to share our sorrows or hardships deeply, the more it becomes a source to overcome the external adversities and trials that come our way. Therefore, the more difficult the external issues are, the more the internal connection must stand in a rewarding position. Then, overcoming the external environment will not be a problem.

However, when the internal connection is weak compared to the external problems faced, overcoming those external problems becomes impossible. It is not uncommon for person A and person B to face the same fate in our daily lives concerning colleagues, relationships, or connections.

From this perspective, if God wishes to establish a relationship with humanity today, in what position will He do so? Will He establish a relationship through superficial words, or will He do so in a serious manner, where He can express historical content that pierces to the bone, in a place where circumstances are understood and emotions are intensified? Establishing a relationship through superficial words may serve as a motive to transcend superficial events, but it cannot be seen as an internal connection that can resolve the serious issues of life and death, which are critical matters that occur only once in a lifetime.

The position of those in the moral world

The providential history of God is not a history meant to resolve individual events. The history of salvation is not about saving an individual, such as a 20-year-old person standing in the position of being 20 years old. When God seeks to save an individual, He places a historical mission upon that person. Even if the person is young, when God needs that young person, it is because there is a divine will to find that young person historically.

When considering the past of a 20-year-old young man, does God wish to establish a relationship with him based on that? No, before discussing the 20 years of his life, God wishes to discuss the origin from which he came, in other words, through his ancestors. When we consider this issue, how shocking would it be if a 20-year-old young man does not know his ancestors? From God's perspective, his ancestors are exceedingly good, so even though he is a young man in his twenties, God knows him and wishes to raise him to fulfill the good deeds of his historical ancestors on this earth. If there is no way to make him understand this mission, how sorrowful would God be? And how shocking would it be for that person standing in that position?

Then, is there a way to know that historical fact? No matter how much a 20-year-old young person struggles alone, he cannot know it by himself. If there were even a book that records the historical content of his good ancestors, that would be one thing, but if there is no such book, what other way is there? If there is a spiritual realm and his good ancestors are there, the only way would be to go to that spiritual realm and meet those good ancestors. Wouldn't that be easier than meeting God, the Lord of Heaven and Earth? That is a given.

Today, in the moral world, those who defend their positions and explain their positions cannot teach the path of morality, just as a 20-year-old young man cannot discern his path. Humanity cannot pursue religion while discussing God from their own positions.

So, from what position should we pursue religion? Is there even a record of such a path historically? Even if there is a record, it cannot be trusted. It cannot be known. So, if God exists, shouldn't we hold onto God? However, God is too far away to grasp.

Therefore, if there are great figures who have shown good deeds before humanity, we can only go to them and ask. If that does not resolve the issue, and if the good ancestors are in the spiritual realm, the only way to solidify our position and find a dignified place is to connect with those in the spiritual realm.

From this perspective, we can see that Eastern thought has vaguely introduced Heaven. It is said, "The good doer will be rewarded by Heaven, and the evil doer will be punished by Heaven." This is vague. It states that if one does good, Heaven will bestow blessings, and if one does evil, it will bring calamity. What is Heaven? Can Eastern thought become a path to connect with God, and can it provide content that teaches us about the God we need and desire in today's society? That is difficult. Prophecy speaks of future points of connection.

When viewed this way, isn't prophecy something that cannot be known until the time comes, even if it establishes future points of connection? Then, isn't today a place that is even less knowable? Therefore, those who seek a solution to these fundamental issues should follow the path of the sages. If there are no sages on this earth, since their destination of good was the end of the world, the eternal world, they should hold onto that path of desire, align themselves with the direction they were heading, and set their wishes in a longer historical direction. Before asking God, if the sages are in the spiritual realm, we can only ask those spirits.

The era of only communicating through truth and words is passing.

Because of such humanity, they did not understand the circumstances under which Jesus earnestly communicated with His disciples before the cross. If you read John chapter 14 in the Bible, you will understand. "I am in you, and you are in me, and I am in the Father, and the Father is in me." This means that you are also in the Father, and the Father is also in you. However, this is something that can only be heard through someone; it is not a direct way to connect with God.

Jesus, who came to this earth, was the greatest among saints. When the disciples, who did not clearly know the direction Jesus was to take, faced the question of how they would walk the path ahead, it was natural that even if they tried, they could not seek the path of Heaven centered on their current selves. Therefore, Jesus, who was facing the final days, could not help but emphasize the way to become one with Him and them. This is an undeniable circumstance.

Even if I go, is there a way for you and me to connect? "There is no other way but to love God with all your heart, all your mind, and all your soul." This was the situation that led Jesus to that conclusion. He also said, "I will go and prepare a place for you and will come again," and "You do not know the way I am going." Moreover, in the path of sincerity, Jesus wished that His disciples would love Him more than their fathers, more than their nations, and more than their wishes or ideals, and that they would live in a realm where their hearts are united and empathized, even if their positions are different. Thus, He said, "You and I are not in different places; we are one. I am in you, and you are in me."

In light of this, the issue is not the letters left behind. The problem lies in the love hidden behind the letters left by Jesus, the heart of love that is of an unknown higher dimension. Centered on that heart, He emphasized the oneness of you and me, not merely the words or the letters left behind. We cannot help but reach that point.

Facing the barrier of death, Jesus, who could not meet or connect with His beloved disciples, was in a poignant position. It is not the words He delivered at that time that are the issue, but rather the fact that He could not say, "Even if you die, die in the place of loving me," knowing that death was imminent for them and that they would have to shed the blood of martyrdom. The unexpressed circumstances and internal connections of Jesus remain in the scriptures. Therefore, the words of truth are not the problem.

Did Jesus say everything He wanted to say in the place of love? Did He say everything He wanted to say in the place of deep love? When we consider this issue, the teachings of the scriptures are not spoken from a place of wanting to love. After expressing all His love, He said, "You should do this..."
The statement made from a commanding position, saying "You must..." is not found anywhere in the Bible. The era in which truth could be conveyed solely through truth is passing. Truth is the true principle and the Word, but we cannot navigate through the era of the Word alone. You must understand this. In the era of the Word, you may encounter the reality, but the love of the reality cannot be conquered. Isn't that right? If you follow the promises of the Word, you may encounter Him, but you cannot conquer His love. There remains work to be done after meeting.

Therefore, the issue is not merely going through the process of the Word but meeting Him and exchanging with each other. Even if I say I love Jesus and He loves me, to what extent did we love each other? "I loved Him in a place where I could die. I was loved in such a place. We swore beyond our circumstances, praised heaven, or sang praises to the ages." Isn't there anyone in our human world who has experienced such a place?

Even the three beloved disciples, what kind of love is that? In the Garden of Gethsemane, faced with death... It was certain that He would die. It was certain that Jesus would die. He was already resolved, having decided to walk the path of death. In such a solemn place, a place that determines life and death, did the three disciples not fall asleep? Not just once. Where could we find the emotional unity of Jesus, who urged them to stay awake and pray two or three times to avoid falling into temptation, on this earth? There was none.

If there had been a disciple who, when He was to walk the final path, said, "I will follow you, for that is my lifelong wish," if there had been such a disciple whom He wanted to love, and if they had parted ways at the place where they would die together, wouldn't He have wanted to say something while carrying the cross towards Golgotha? Wouldn't the story He wanted to tell, which transcended the fear of death, have appeared in human history? However, because their stories were different, due to that divergence, humanity could not inherit the heavenly story that could overcome death on that solemn path. Therefore, we cannot help but think about how tragic that fact is.

When we consider this, we can understand that the path of virtue cannot be resolved by itself, nor can it be resolved by the authority or power of any church established in that environment. Therefore, we must find a way to resolve the higher inner connection through the founder, whether it is the church leader or another. And how will we guide the direction for the religious people today, who have lost their way and do not even know the direction they should go? You may think of this issue indifferently, but when considered seriously, it cannot be anything less than a historical issue of world significance.

The suffering of a sovereign trying to determine the rise and fall of a nation is great, yet if there is anyone on this earth who is striving to establish the foundation for the victory of virtue for the liberation of all nations, that person would be a great individual. On the other hand, he must stand in a position that is more solemn than anyone else and go through the process of pursuing the urgent problems of life. When we think of this fact, we can say that until that position is resolved, he is the most pitiful person.

Until such a being appears on this earth, the historical extension of humanity will continue, and we are in a situation where the new ideals that humanity hopes for cannot be realized. Not only for nation-states but through the world, we have already tried everything. We have tried with power, we have tried with the capabilities of materialism, which claimed material supremacy, and we have mobilized all human wisdom and knowledge to the highest degree, but we have entered a stage where we recognize that there can be no second liberation of humanity. So, having tried with material and having tried with people, what is left that we have not yet tried? Only love remains.

What do people desire? They desire material. They desire dignity. Then, after having money and becoming educated, what do they want to do? They want to make the world their stage and live traveling with those they love. Isn't that the desire of humanity? In order to fulfill such a straightforward desire, humanity has tried with material and through all human wisdom and authority, but they have faced failure. Now, if there is one thing left to try, it is love. There is only one path to try with the history of love.

Then, where will that love arise? That is the question. Where will that love begin? Until now, we have claimed material centered on humanity and the authority of humanity. We have centered on love between humans until now. That will not work. If it cannot work, what will we do? If there is a path of love here, humanity must yearn for it. The solution to the issue of young people in their twenties, as mentioned earlier, can only come if God intervenes or if the ancestors who know that history intervene. There are only these two options. In this sense, we need God, and we need our ancestors.

From this perspective, what is the core of the teachings of the Unification Church? It is to regard God as our parent, to recognize Him as the fundamental parent of humanity, and to seek Him as the source of our hearts. Then what do we want to do? We want to seek our ancestors. Here we find the point of convergence. This is what the Unification Church desires. Because we have fallen parents, having been born as descendants of false parents, we deny this and reject the historical reality that has been established on a global scale. Under the origin of love centered on God, we seek the true parents of humanity in a relative position that receives the unified love of God. This is the ultimate destination the Unification Church must pursue, and this should be the emotional life of the members of the Unification Church.

From this perspective, today the Unification Church is not discussing emotional issues centered on humanity on this earth, but is in a position to discuss the emotional history centered on our ancestors from heaven, so you must understand that we are looking toward the world of the heart. We must establish a relationship with God's heart. We must create the world of the heart. That is a different dimension. It is different from the conventional dimension. This is an innovative dimension, a higher dimension. What has started from there is not a flat emotion but has started with a three-dimensional emotional content.

Because of this, this is the final hope that humanity must converge upon, and no matter how difficult the path may be, it can only be a point that can lead all miserable histories to happiness. If that does not come to fruition, no matter how happy the process is, no matter how true the process is, and no matter what we have in the process, if the final destination cannot resolve the issues between God, who is the foundation of heaven and earth, and us, then all of that will be in vain.

That is why the Bible concludes simply to love God and to love Jesus. Who is Jesus? What kind of being did He come as? He came as the Son of God, the only begotten Son. And as the only begotten Son, He received love. He was the only begotten Son who could finally receive God's love. Who else could receive all the love of the parents but the only son?

From this perspective, the name "only begotten Son" in the history of Christianity is a great word. Isn't it? He is the only begotten Son, so how much must God have loved Him to call Him the only begotten Son? In the past, God directly created the ancestors of humanity, Adam and Eve, but could He not love them all and did He not take them away from the embrace of love? But who could take away a person who receives the love of the Absolute Being among the love of the Absolute Being? No one can take them away. Therefore, there cannot be a fall. The fall occurred because, in a desperate situation, the object of love was not possessed. Thus, having reached this point, in other words, because He came from a position that has experienced a love greater than that of the fallen ancestors, He becomes qualified to emerge as the ancestor of humanity's hope centered on love. That is the Messiah. Therefore, outside of the path through the Messiah, outside of the path through Jesus, there is no solution to human problems. That is why Jesus could conclude, "I am the way, the truth, and the life; no one comes to the Father except through me." Our Unification Church aims to overcome that.

When I ask where I came from, most people say I am a monkey's offspring, a monkey's offspring. Are you a monkey's offspring? In today's communist logic, it is said that humans have become human through labor, developing their rights of recognition and standing on an accumulated foundation of knowledge... So, are we monkeys? The dimension is different.

That is why we emphasize the theory of human nature in Unification Thought. Humans are fundamentally different in nature. Humans are of a different seed. Fundamentally different. Children already possess the nature to distinguish between good and evil. They will naturally come to know this without knowing the constitution or attending school. Today, humans do not clearly know their origin. They do not know whether they started from God or from humans. We are the same. You were born by your mother and father, but as soon as you were born, you think you are alone. You came out alone... From the perspective of being alone, you wonder where you came from. However, they do not know that history. So, they think whatever they want. Since there is no foundation for thought, they think according to their whims, concluding, "It must be like this. It must be like that," but they cannot arrive at a conclusion of "It is so." However, even though they have their own experiences of growing up and loving, if someone says, "Your father and mother do not exist," even if they are dead, they would immediately respond, "Hey, you little brat, why don't they exist?" The power that can transcend history
Even among fallen humans, there are instances where a father and son are separated and then meet again as adults due to some reason, which you may have seen in movies. Isn't it the duty of a parent to overcome suffering to find their child? The child does not think about it at all.

"I lacked in loving your father (or mother). What is my regret at this moment of passing? When you think that you must hold onto your beloved ones and your beloved children, the encounter of your will with us must not end in sorrow.

The footsteps you took to find this poor Republic of Korea and this people must not end in sorrow. Father, are there children who take pride in knowing that only the group of unification can know such content? When we look at the morning sunlight, we must feel that the sunlight is different from the sunlight we saw in the past. When we breathe in new air, we must think that it is air different from the past. We must feel that the steps we take today are different from the steps we took yesterday, and we must become sons and daughters who can add progressive, weighty, and three-dimensional stories, capable of pledging to ourselves.

Father, please lead your many children scattered across the nation. Their hearts are centered on you, so please move them through their nature so that they can align with the gentle direction of your providence. If they deviate from that direction, even if it means striking us, please allow us to go the way we must go, even if it means rearranging our environment.

The Unification Church must go. The Unification Church must establish your will according to that will. Therefore, we must continue on the path that has been busy and restless until now. We must go together with you. We must go because your wish is so. We must go because your request is so.

Father, even if the path we walk is not smooth and your wish becomes heavier, if you can truly command us to "endure the path you can endure with all your strength," then there are not just one or two sons and daughters here who wish to go through that place, but as the number increases, we feel that the foundation of your comfort expands. Therefore, I earnestly ask and wish that you allow us to be a group that can follow along with what you desire.

We must become like children. We must long for the honey of truth, yearn for the embrace of love, and be like children who can long for your face that looks upon us with hope and welcomes us. I earnestly ask you to allow us to be such children. At this time, please be with us in your will, and allow today to be a day that aligns with your will, and allow our understanding to align with your will.

I once again ask you to allow us to be a group of unification that can fully fulfill our responsibilities centered on your will in 1972, and I offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.

The human heart pursuing a better world
We know that in our daily lives, we experience many ups and downs. At times, we blame ourselves for not achieving our intended goals, feeling despondent or in despair, yet even in such moments, we either resolve to make a new determination ourselves or are led by the encouragement of peers, mentors, or seniors to stand in a position where we receive new stimulation and reaffirm our wishes. We know that we are living lives filled with such fluctuations. Therefore, even if there are people who possess themselves, we understand through our life experiences that it is not something that can last.

Just as it is for an individual, the same applies to a family where many people live together. When all the members of that family unite for the purpose of that family or hope for its well-being and invest new strength into it, that family will make new advancements with meaningful significance. However, if the central parents are lax, or if the parents are not lax but the children are in conflict, that family will inevitably show a different form than it did yesterday. Even if it was a hopeful family until yesterday, if it encounters such results today, we know all too well that it cannot escape becoming a sorrowful family.

When we think of a family in that way, the same applies to a nation or a people. When we look at the Republic of Korea, there is undoubtedly a path that the Republic of Korea must take. Although humans may not understand well, there is no doubt that there is a place of hope that this Republic of Korea must reach beyond its current situation.

To establish a confident direction centered on that will, it must be united from the sovereign above to the people below, and that direction must be aligned. When we move toward a place where we can encourage each other, the nation of the Republic of Korea will become a nation where hope can come.

However, when the upper side asserts its position and the lower side asserts its position, causing them to diverge, no matter how good that hope may be, it will inevitably retreat and cannot avoid falling apart. Before we can recover that fallen position and find a place where we can resolve ourselves even more than before, we cannot restore that fallen position.

We can observe the path that the Republic of Korea takes by reflecting on our individual lives. The same goes for the fate of the world. However, because we have the responsibility to open the door of the world and must proceed directly, we are in a position where we must touch everything. 

Nevertheless, since we must take responsibility for this work without the environmental resources of human and material resources, we must receive your compassion like a madman. That is the only way to survive, so we have led the Unification Church until today with a heart that fears your compassion may leave us. 

Therefore, please do not allow the Unification Church to be one that turns away with tears of sorrow and curses. Even if it is heartbreaking and unjust, if there is even one person who cannot stay in this place, saying, "I cannot remain without holding your hand," this place can remain a foundation of hope, and the nation and the world can again be sacrificed. We know that it is our responsibility to open that path, so even if it is a pitiful Unification Church, it is fine. Even if the whole world criticizes the Unification Church, it is fine. Even if this nation persecutes the Unification Church, it is fine. Even if all people in the world shoot harsh arrows at the Unification Church, it is fine. 

However, we must become a Unification Church that cannot be abandoned by you. Even if no one welcomes me, if I am a Unification Church member welcomed only by you, that is enough. Please allow this heart to remain steadfast and unwavering. Thus, we must bloom the flower of loyalty and offer the fragrance of incense before you, leaving everything in your memory, and we must become a group that can trace the path of such a life. 

Father, as I reflect from the time I was ignorant until now, there are many stories. Even if those stories disappear like clouds, let us remember the unforgettable historical sad facts that are engraved in your bones during the historical era. Because we did not know that, even if I forget my sorrow, I can inherit your sorrowful appearance, inherit your bloodline, inherit your circumstances, and inherit the world of your wishes. This is the absolute wish of the Unification Church believers, so please allow us to be a group that can stand in that place, Father. 

Please wait for us. Father, we must pray. We must pray, "Please have compassion on the fate of this nation." I must not become a pitiful person who prays to ask you to wait for my personal concerns from a place of urgency. Unification Church members must not do that. Please wait. 

Wasn’t it the desperate situation of Jesus in the Garden of Gethsemane, who blocked the fate of the nation and the world, saying, "Strike me"? "Not my will, but your will be done," as he fell, holding onto the future will that could remain for future generations, even if he perished? We long for the heart of Jesus and wish to be a Unification Church that can keep that position. 

It is not a problem for us to live miserably and die miserably. Our wish is that our descendants do not stand in such a position, so please allow us to be a group that can leave this absolute principle until the end. 

Heaven, now, centered on August 30, the time for the North and South to exchange is approaching, so please bring heavenly blessings there. Let it be a crossroads that can bring the fortune of spring to the winter garden, and please allow it to be a starting point for the liberation of this nation and this people. 

Just as Abel went to find Cain, let all those who go to find… Knowing that the principle is to go from above and below, please do not let them become a group that goes with means and tricks, but let them be a group that can find the way to establish your will. The world is paying attention through this period, so please allow a new path to open that can boast of the sovereignty of this nation and this people. 

Also, since you know the time we desire, I earnestly ask you to allow the day of liberation and unification to come, where this nation and this people can enjoy the victory of the path beyond the suffering you desire. 

Please correct the spirit of this nation so that it can go to the world, and let it walk the path of rest where you can rest, as a day of victory, glory, and pride, so that it can leave a spirit of the nation that can be praised and boasted before all people. 

This morning, please allow your young children to know a new path in their hearts and let it be a foundation of resolution on their life journey. I earnestly ask and pray all these things in the name of True Parents. Amen. 

3) What are you doing? 

I am grateful that we have gathered here in good health after much hard work in the local areas. We have now passed the very hot peak. Since you have come here this evening, I hope that the next five days will be a period of re-determination, keeping in mind the tasks we must undertake for new activities. 

Today, I would like to talk briefly on the topic, "What are you doing?" 

To inherit true history… 

You have a history of activities since entering the Unification Church. Also, looking at the teacher himself, there is a history of leading the Unification Church until now. And when we look at God centered on Him, God also has a similar history. Greatly centered on heaven…
There is such a history, and a historical connection remains for people who represent the land. Here, the small must be absorbed around the larger and the larger must reveal greater value, which is our principle. 

From this perspective, looking at the history of the Unification Church, the history of the Teacher is compounded here. Furthermore, since the Unification Church began to reveal itself to the world, on August 13, 1972, at the Cheongpyeong Training Center. 
* This statement was made at the first national church leaders' retreat, and according to the order, it should have been included in Volume 60, but due to editorial issues, it was included in Volume 61.

Here, your history is attached. When we center on the history of the Unification Church, we can say that on earth, the history of the Teacher and your history are attached. However, when we view it centered on God, we must understand that the entirety of God's history is included here. 

So, what must the Unification Church do to have a true history? The history that the Unification Church has achieved on earth alone cannot become a true history. The subject of truth is ultimately God, so to establish a true history, we must establish God above all else. Therefore, we, who represent the land, must determine how to inherit the heavenly tradition centered on God, the center of truth. Only then can we inherit the true history. Ultimately, to inherit the true history, it concludes that we must inherit God's traditional history. 

To transfer God's traditional history to earth, when viewed in light of the restoration providence, it requires a point of resolution centered on the present, but the motivation for that resolution is connected to the history of all ages. In other words, because the ancestors of humanity fell, the restoration history must be repeated to overcome that fallen point. The foundation for overcoming that critical path is not heaven, but the earth. Therefore, it cannot be done solely by God. It must be done with a focus on people, carrying out that history (role). 

In carrying out that history centered on people, since it started from the fallen Adam and Eve, the standard of the original parents who did not fall must be completed. The issue is how to horizontally adapt God's will and the unfallen value standards centered on those parents to the entire world. To do this, God's traditional history must be transferred to earth. For that, parents who are greater than the fallen parents must emerge. 

Moreover, after that, the fallen descendants emerged and rebelled against God, flourishing the world of evil, so unfallen descendants must come forth to eliminate the flourishing world of evil. This compounded mission lies with us today, who are responsible for the restoration providence. 

From this perspective, for each of us, the questions of "What should I do?" and "What should I do?" cannot help but arise. Each of you must have the personality to assert yourselves. You all have your own opinions. You have lived through your own history and have your own worldview. However, the question is whether the history you have lived centered on yourself has become a history that can inherit the tradition of God's restoration providence, and whether the living environment you are currently in serves as a standard that can fulfill and indemnify the overall will of the restoration providence on this earthly foundation. This is a serious issue. 

We ourselves are individuals, but we are individuals who have inherited the will of our parents. Here, those parents must be parents who hope for historical good standards. Each of us must be in the position of the descendants of parents who have fulfilled historical aspirations. When viewed in this way, the question of whether such people exist is a serious issue. 

Jesus, who came as a representative capable of inheriting God's historical tradition, when you look at yourselves, some have spent ten years in the Unification Church, and others have spent several years, and all of you are in that situation. In your historical faith life, the question arises as to whether you have lived a history that aligns with the traditional standards that God desires. If you examine and critique this closely, you cannot deny that you have lived through a conflicting historical past. Furthermore, regarding the present life you are living, if you critically evaluate whether there are members who possess a lifestyle that can align with the traditional standards desired by God, this is a significant issue. 

When viewed in this way, there is an inevitable divergence between God's desired position regarding humanity and today's humanity's desired position regarding God. While God has a tradition of "this is how it should be," today's humanity seeks to go based on secular habits, personal desires, and individual-centered ambitions. The greater the divergence, the more God's suffering is involved, and it is undeniable that an indemnity content is required. 

So, where can we condense one aspect of such content? We can condense it between Jesus and God. Setting ourselves aside, since we are in a position where we cannot inherit God's tradition, when we look at Jesus as the representative who can inherit all of God's historical tradition, we can see that the desires of God and Jesus are also at odds. 

The prayer in Gethsemane with dual meanings 
What is the title of Jesus' prayer as he spent the night praying in Gethsemane before the issue of the cross? It is "Not my will, but Yours be done." Here, the will has dual meanings. When looking at Jesus himself, he is a person who came for the will. He is a person centered on the will. Therefore, he should have inherited all of God's traditional historical connections and should have formed a horizontal relationship in the present age according to those connections. He should not have been in any position other than the will. Yet, why did he say "my will"? When considering this issue, we must recognize that there is certainly a conflicting content involved. 

So, what position does Jesus occupy? It is not a position representing the individual. Is it merely a position of Jesus sent to this earth? No, it is a position representing the nation and the people. If all the high priests of the Jewish sect could not fulfill their duties, Jesus had to stand in a position where he could fulfill them all. 

From that perspective, we must recognize that Jesus, who knows God's inner circumstances, faced a great conflict. Why? Because he must follow the path that can align with God, yet that path is too far from this human world. If he were to deny his own position as one who must gather humanity and fulfill the will, he would not know, but if he denies it, he cannot have hope. Therefore, we can think that Jesus, who faced that position as a representative of humanity, could not help but think of "my will" before God. 

Jesus, who knows all the circumstances and conditions of humanity, wanted to acknowledge the human situation, but it was in the opposite direction of God's higher will, with a 180-degree difference. From that perspective, Jesus, wanting to align with God's will and direction, must have had a desire for something that could adjust that as much as possible. As the responsible leader representing the world, he could not help but have such a heart. 

However, in the end, at the critical moment where no adjustment or compromise could be made, he said, "Not my will, but Yours be done." At that moment, he had to deny his own will and seek the will of the Father. In the position of having the fallen nation of Israel behind him, and with the Jewish faith that could destroy the history of God's 4,000 years of effort in a moment, while praying earnestly in Gethsemane, Jesus must have wanted to listen to all the human circumstances and appeal to God with all the plans he could to restore humanity. 

Therefore, the time he spent praying, bringing up the historical mistakes of his ancestors before God, and looking at the current position of the Israelite nation that could not fulfill its responsibilities, must have been a time of deep pain as he examined the inner circumstances and reported them to God. Knowing all these circumstances, he wanted to express and understand that will, but in the end, he was in a position where he could not help but rely on God's decision. Therefore, Jesus, who came to find the land, stood in a position where he could not abandon his mission to save all nations and peoples, and he could not help but utter the decisive statement, "Not my will, but Yours be done." How serious must that position have been? 

For Jesus, standing in that position, the question of "What should I do?" was unavoidable. "What will you do with the Jewish faith and the Israelite nation that you have worked for over 4,000 years? I have come to take on the central mission, but now I am in a position where I cannot fulfill that responsibility, so what should I do?" This is what he could only ask. At that moment, we must discover that Jesus was groaning under the most unbearable suffering in his heart. 

If there were a way to embrace that inner situation and resolve it, if there were a way for that story to connect, Jesus must have had a strong desire to seek that way, and thus he prayed to God, "Not my will, but Yours be done." How painful and serious must that position have been? However, the disciples at that time could not have imagined it. 

When we focus on the issue of "What should I do?" from the perspective of the Messiah, who was in an intermediary position, and when we consider the problem of "What will you do?" rather than "What should I do?", we must recognize that Jesus did not want to discuss his own circumstances. He set aside his own position and thought, "Isn't it my purpose to first resolve your situation, the situation of the one who sent me?" 

Because this emotional connection existed between God's heart and Jesus' heart, when Jesus said, "Even if I enter a position where I can perish, I can still establish a new Israel," he was able to stimulate God to make a new resolution. In other words, the motivation that arose to resurrect the dying Jesus and to make a new resolution came from that moment. In that serious position, he faced the inner question of "What will you do?" and denied his own will, preparing to find a way that could please God and allow God to rest. This became the motivation that could establish a new starting point for the victorious history of Christianity on this earth, which no one welcomed. 

From this perspective, what is the mission of our Unification Church today? It is not simply a movement centered on a new ideology inherited from the historical tradition centered around a certain individual in the Unification Church. It began with God. It started from God. So, it began with God being present. The God who is the Creator, who has been creating since the beginning of creation, who has been overcoming difficult problems with the desire to fulfill the ideal of creation, all of this should have been realized through Adam and Eve. However, Adam and Eve completely shattered this. 

Considering the heart of God the Father, who is in that position, and thinking about the position of the wounded Father centered on His heart, "How do You feel?" we must think about Jesus' heart. What can we compare that to? Because of these two, a foundation of happiness could have been established in heaven and earth, and the realization of the ideal that the Creator desires could have been possible. Yet, witnessing the entire situation falling apart, what must have been God's heart? This is a serious issue. 

Those of you who have experience raising beloved children will understand, but when it comes to the future of your children, if you think, "This child will surely succeed globally. A glorious position is secured. It is guaranteed. It is undoubtedly decisive," and then in the process of heading toward that decisive course, if everything is completely cut off, what would happen? For someone experiencing such a scene, the hope they had longed for becomes their enemy. Isn't that so? What was established as God's ideal becomes a condition for hope and a stimulating factor for happiness, but instead, it becomes a cause for lamentation, putting God in a position of being shot at by that lamentation. What would God have felt in that position? This is a serious issue. What must God have felt witnessing Adam's fall? It cannot be a trivial matter. 

Even this morning, I briefly spoke about something similar, but when someone experiences sadness, to comfort that person, one must either have a sadder experience or love them more or have a connection from a higher position.
114   What will you do?
You must be in a position of defeat. Without that, you cannot completely remove the sad story and make them happy. Isn’t that right, everyone? 
Or when looking at emotional issues in married life, there is no one to comfort during a couple's fight. There is no one to stop it. You cannot intervene without having deeper emotional content. However, when a parent who loves their children with a love greater than that of the couple comes and discusses from the standpoint of loving their children, they will be intervened. If you approach with a more loving and valuable content that allows you to go beyond the sad events and be joyful, it can be comforting, but with anything less, it cannot provide comfort. Isn’t this the fallen emotion of our humanity? 
In this light, is there anything that can comfort God’s heart as He looks at the fallen Adam and Eve right after the fall? Absolutely not. If there is someone who is in a position to be loved more than Adam and Eve, someone who is in a higher position than Adam and Eve and can please God, then perhaps, but without that, there is no way to comfort God. 
So, is there anyone among the fallen humans today who has a deeper emotional connection than Adam and Eve? Such a person can come and comfort God, who was saddened by the historical wounds of Adam and Eve right after the fall, but without that, it cannot be done. 
When Jesus prayed, “Abba Father, not my will, but yours be done,” what does this distance signify? Isn’t it a resolution that Jesus expressed not to walk the same path as the history of fallen Adam? Because he thought of himself in emotional issues, didn’t he completely deny himself? Didn’t he deny all his environmental conditions? 
From this perspective, he is better than Adam. He is better than Adam. Isn’t he the one who sought God’s inner connection with a heart that can be better than Adam? The tears he shed while praying there were not just tears of sorrow; he felt a sorrow greater than that of Adam and Eve being cast out, shedding tears and blood, and because of that, he could become a motive to forget the historical origin of the fall. However, anything less than that cannot suffice. 
The historical mission of the Unification Church 
If we acknowledge that this is the traditional history in the emotional world, then those belonging to the Unification Church today must change. The Unification Church today is not just inheriting the history that Jesus failed. It aims for a higher, shining victory. This applies to the individual, the family, and even beyond the nation, state, and world; isn’t this the historical mission that the Unification Church must bear? When you recognize this, the problem becomes significant. 
From this perspective, you are witnessing the downfall of the nation. You are witnessing the downfall of the people. Today, we are witnessing the downfall of our tribe. We are witnessing the downfall of our families, and the downfall of your sons and daughters. If it were something that could automatically recover according to cyclical laws after a time passes, I wouldn’t worry. However, the more it declines, the further away it becomes. 
When you stand in a position to witness this and take on the responsibility as a young man with the spirit of Jesus, how will you view the Garden of Gethsemane? Was it merely the Garden of Gethsemane that Jesus visited 2,000 years ago? No. A position greater than that of Jesus praying in the Garden of Gethsemane 2,000 years ago is needed. 
When you look at yourself, when you try to stay up all night, did you have companions around you who could cry with you and stay up all night together? Did you have anyone who could be your colleague? When you consider these issues, even though you are in a position to pursue valuable goals better than Jesus, if you stand in a position worse than Jesus, what will happen to God, who is wounded as the emotional subject? This cannot be a trivial matter. When you think of God’s heart, who had to push His beloved son to the cross to die after making a decision through negotiation, how can we stand in a position worse than Jesus? What will happen to God then? 
Self-centeredness leads to ruin 
When Jesus heard from Mary that the wine had run out at the wedding in Cana of Galilee, and said, “Woman, what does this have to do with me?” it may seem like a flat statement or a hurtful remark in the context of the mother-son relationship inherited from Israel's traditional history, but it is a dignified statement when viewed from the moment the heavenly principle is overturned. If that mother is in a position to betray and ruin the heavenly principle, she is not just a woman but the worst of the worst. If you simply acknowledge such a mother, wouldn’t your wife and children also follow suit? 
In this sense, Jesus did well not to marry. He did well. If he had taken a wife who opposed his will, what would he have done? When Mary herself, who knew that Jesus was born to fulfill God’s will, failed to align her inner heart with that, what would happen if he had married a woman who was not of the same mind? Would that wife’s relatives side with Jesus or with the wife? What do you think? They would side with the wife. Then what would happen to that lineage? That lineage would also side with the wife. If children were born, it would be reasonable for them to side with Jesus, but what if they opposed him? 
Do you think God wouldn’t have worried about such issues as the subject who promotes the heavenly providence? People repeatedly fall and weave history around themselves, living centered on themselves. When God, who knows this reality well, sees that the counterpart who met Jesus is trying to make Jesus their husband from a self-centered perspective, it will all lead to ruin. If a child desires a relationship with a father based on self-centered values, it will all lead to ruin. So, is this love issue easy? 
The subject’s will must be central to the circumstances 
Now, from this perspective, you have received a blessing centered on tremendous issues. The standard of blessing you know is not something that has come through countless sacrifices in the history of heaven. Is it a blessing that you can know and feel from such a position? Is it God’s desire for the families of the Unification Church to be established on the customary standards of dealing with men and women? This is something you need to reconsider. 
If you had a wife, the question would arise, “What should we do in front of the will? What should we do?” When you look at it from the perspective of your original heart, the question becomes, “What about our family? What about my children?” This is the issue. It’s not about not being able to feed them. It’s not about not being able to clothe them. The only issue is the will that must be left behind. 
To restore the fallen Adam, God sent Jesus after 4,000 years of history to indemnify this, but thinking about God’s heartbreaking situation, who abandoned the ideal of the completion of the restoration of spirit and body and buried the idea of physical restoration while only pursuing the idea of spiritual restoration, is not something we can merely conceptually understand. When we think of a father standing in the position of “this is the reality,” how astonishing it must be to realize that there is such a God. 
From this perspective, what will you do? When you think about people like me, families like mine, couples like mine, what will you do? The only way to proceed is through judgment. The only way to proceed is through punishment. The only way to proceed is through the final ultimatum. Isn’t that something you can accept? You must acknowledge it. It should be natural. Jesus, who wanted to save the Israelite people, acknowledged that the nation must perish and held onto the Israelite people. He acknowledged that it could perish and prayed while holding onto Judaism. It’s the same here. 
Then, even if you cannot pray the negotiation prayer like Jesus for the nation, have you done so centered on your family? Have you done it centered on your children and your wife? When you look at your family and consider the question of what to do, realizing that you cannot leave behind a historical legacy for the nation and people, how can you simply wish to sweep this away with your own hands and want to live under the flames of curses from heaven? Isn’t it something that should be felt continuously as a deep sorrow? 
Whether it’s your family or the Unification Church, when you say, “Father, what will you do in the future? What about me?” the circumstances are different. They are different. The circumstances that God sees and the circumstances that you see are different. When you say, “My circumstances are like this, so what should I do?” it is different for every person. Unity cannot exist under such circumstances. It does not connect. That is an absolute denial from the very beginning. It cannot be. However, when you consider the question of what you will do centered on the will of the subject, then the circumstances connect. Shouldn’t it be that way? 
In that regard, the position of “not my will, but yours be done” is a harsh position. There is a parent’s heart wanting to save their child, but wasn’t it a scene where they had to turn their face away? Wasn’t it a position where they could not respond in a straightforward manner to their beloved spouse, parents, or anyone with whom they have a vertical relationship? 
The history of a new tradition can only unfold in the emotional world 
So, where do you intend to establish such a will? Do you intend to establish it in the position of “What will God do?” or in the position of “What will I do?” It’s the same. The position where Jesus stood and the position where we stand today are the same. 
From this perspective, Jesus had to be prepared to sacrifice in order to leave a place where both he and God could stand. I love God more than Adam does, and I feel more pity for the mistakes Adam made than anyone else. Isn’t He in a more difficult position than I am, having not abandoned me? Therefore, when he says, “What happened is not my fault but the fault of the nation. The nation has forsaken it, and humanity has forsaken it. So please strike me in place of humanity,” a new history of emotional revival begins from here. 
For example, let’s say Adam and Eve fell, and Adam has a younger brother. When that younger brother sees God driving out the fallen Adam and Eve, he might say, “Parents! Please do not drive out my older brother and sister; I will take that path, so strike me instead.” If he holds onto his parents like that, a new path can emerge from here. What kind of history is that? It is the history of Abel. “Even if my parents’ hearts are more painful and unjust than those of my sinful older siblings, I will overcome that and take responsibility, so please place all burdens on me. Not only the cross of my siblings but also the cross of my parents, please place it all on me.” If there is a son who can say this, God will shed tears of compassion because of that son. It is possible. In this world, if there is an unfilial child, and his younger brother stands before the parents, feeling more pain than the parents themselves, and says, “I will sincerely accept any difficulties that come my way,” a new tradition can emerge. This can only happen in the emotional world. It is impossible in the world of reason and logic. 
The history of Abel 
To establish this traditional history, this emotional path, and to overturn the path of the fall, it cannot be done with Adam or Eve. If there is another younger brother, or someone who says they will step forward into a position more miserable than the father, more miserable than the son, then God cannot strike him, so He forgives him. Isn’t that the history of Abel? When we think that God had no other choice but to leave such a history, we can indeed discuss here that God is love. We cannot deny the principle that it can only be resolved through the history of love. That is the history of Abel. 
So, who is Abel? He is the son who stands in the position to take responsibility for God’s sorrow, as another Cain or another Adam. The one who historically represents Adam and bears fruit is Jesus. That is why Jesus took on the responsibility of both. “Strike me in place of the nation and the world.” This is Jesus’ situation. “Not my will, but yours be done. I will bear all of the Father’s pain and continue the lineage from here.” Wasn’t this the position of Jesus? From here, history moves in a new direction… We cannot deny that a new direction and factors were pioneered from here. 
When we view this as the traditional history of Abel, which has a pure origin that has passed through the historical era, indeed, we, the members of the Unification Church, stand before this solemn 6,000-year history… 6,000 years, you say? But is it really just 6,000 years? Before such history, can we stand with a pure heart that has a deeper emotional connection than the Messiah? The Messiah played such games while having three disciples behind him, but if he could do so while having the nation and family behind him, would that be unfortunate? It may seem unfortunate, but it is not. Would those who participated, like Peter, John, and James, become unfortunate? It may seem unfortunate and miserable to stand in that position, but it is not miserable, nor is it unfortunate. Could it not be a factor of happiness? History would have unfolded as a brilliant history of victory because of them, a different direction of Christian history. It is the same. It is the same. 
Then, from such a position, if you can say, “Not my will, but yours be done,” and place parents in that position instead of Peter, John, and James, and hold onto the nation and appeal, or hold onto the people and take responsibility for the fate of your future will, God will not abandon you.
How much will you expect? "Because of you, a new wish will be fulfilled." This will be said. It is, of course, the history of Abel that can love and shine, in other words, it can bloom and reveal its beauty all around, and it is a good chance to emit the fragrance contained in the flowers all around. Isn't it true that a rose must be touched to release its fragrance? The same principle applies here.

A way for unification to emerge
From this perspective... everyone, the Republic of Korea is currently divided between the North and the South. There are two diverging paths, one heading South and the other heading North, with different purposes. When we look at the issue of how unification will occur, it is serious. Who will take on the subjective mission? If South Korea takes it on, North Korea will oppose it, and if North Korea takes it on, South Korea will oppose it. If one insists on its own position, it will inevitably lead to a breakdown.

The question is how to resolve this. The problem is that a Korean who loves North Korea more than anyone from South Korea must emerge. As long as there is someone who loves North Korea more than North Koreans love it, there is no other way to seek a solution. When there is someone who is more patriotic than anyone in South Korea and more patriotic than anyone in North Korea, then a way for unification can emerge from there. Is there any other way? No matter how much I think about it, isn't there no other way?

Then what about this nation? In this country, which is bordered left and right by the 38th parallel, when those standing on that line are members of our Unification Church, what should we do? This is the problem. The issue is how to resolve the problem. It is to suffer more than North Koreans and more than South Koreans. How do we bring forth a super-national patriotism established through such suffering? This is the shortcut and solution to saving Korea. This is how it is viewed. Unifying the evil world and the good world is the same. A loyal subject greater than the loyal subjects of the evil world must emerge. Until now, those who have aimed for goodness must have someone who can claim loyalty greater than the loyalty established by our ancestors to restore the broken history.

In that sense, Jesus was great. You cannot win with a faction that fights against each other. The way for God and the Israelite people is to die for God and die for the people. Isn't that the way of the cross? In loving humanity, he loved more than anyone throughout history, and in loving God, he loved more than anyone throughout history. Therefore, the history that was destined to perish took a new direction and advanced into the world of purpose, which is the Christian cultural sphere. That is a historical fact.

From this perspective, is the Unification Church you believe in and are moving within truly the Unification Church in its true sense? How is it? Is the person leading you, the leader of the Unification Church, truly your leader in the true sense? When we consider the starting point from which he can say, "This is a new stepping stone," based on where he is, we must become those who can praise victory and sing of the peaceful kingdom. We must stand in a position more miserable than two worlds, where everything can collapse, where everything can become treacherous, yet we must become a group that can consistently preserve the beauty of loyalty on the historical path.

When I think about this, the Unification Church of the 1960s is a thing of the past. At that time, the Unification Church could not stand in a position to ask, "What shall we do for the nation?" Back then, the issue was "What shall we do for myself?" but now the dimension is different. In the 1970s, didn't we enter an era where we ask, "Father, what shall we do for this nation?" <Words> We know that there is a gap between people in the history of our fallen humanity. This gap began with Adam and Eve and has grown through history among countless tribes and nations. 

Not only is there a gap between humans, but there is also a wall between God and us. We also recognize that a wall has arisen between God, the subject of good, and the evil spirits that oppose good from the standpoint of evil. We understand that due to the fall, the fate of unity has not been realized in this universe or heaven and earth. Even when we look at ourselves as individuals, we see that there is a gap between our hearts and bodies. The question of how to unify the heart and body has been the foundation of humanity's historical efforts, and we know that history is still progressing in one direction to resolve this issue. We live in such a position. We embrace such a self as we live.

The path to unity must begin with the individual.
Today, the world longs for peace. All people dream of a unified ideal world. This ideal world cannot be achieved without going through each individual. We cannot reach that world without securing the foundation of ideals and expanding that environment through each individual.

When we think this way, the question arises: where should we welcome the day of unity? In this end time of history, can we welcome that day centered on the world? The more we ponder this, the more we conclude that it is impossible. Furthermore, when we consider whether it is possible centered on nations, it is also impossible. When we look at a society, we see that there is competition among them. There are conflicts among them. Even when we focus on families, we know there are customs that take conflicting positions. 

Moreover, when we see that our own bodies and hearts are in conflict, we realize that the path to peace and unity cannot be sought elsewhere but must be explored within ourselves. Unless some individual completely represents heaven, earth, nations, or specific families, or all humanity to form a unified entity, we cannot see the beginning of unity.
