<Words> Human beings are living their lives in search of their own purpose. Regardless of age, young or old, we know that humanity is struggling to find its own path in life. Individuals are in such a position, and at the same time, families are also following their own paths. Broadening the scope, nations and ethnic groups are also pursuing their own paths. The same goes for the world. In other words, as long as humanity remains, there is a path that must be followed as human beings. Not only is there a path for humanity alone, but if there is a heavenly principle, there must also be a path that heavenly principle must follow. In this light, if God exists, there must be a path that God desires to take. Perhaps there is an inevitable path that God wishes to walk alongside humanity.

Individuals have struggled to find a point of purpose where heart and body are in harmony. When we look at an individual, we know that they have both a heart and a body. Therefore, there is a path that the body wishes to take, and a path that the heart wishes to take. When one follows the path desired by the body, they will find themselves facing purposes that conflict with the heart, and they will inevitably encounter such a conclusion. Conversely, if one follows the heart, they will be able to move toward the destination the heart desires. When we consider that this conflicting position is the state of each individual human being, we realize that the collective appearance of such individuals forms the world.

Thus, there are those in the world who follow the path of the external world, and there are those who follow the path of the internal world. Those who follow the path of the internal world are the people of the democratic world, while those who follow the path of the external world are the people of the communist world. 

Where do the internal and external standards originate? They originate from the individual known as "I." We should unite around "I," but because the purposes of the body and the heart are separated from "I," humanity and the world are ultimately heading towards the endpoints of two different worlds, which we must face directly. 

So what is my will? It is neither the path that the external body follows nor the path that follows the internal heart's will. What is that will? It is a path that must be followed centered around a value-oriented purpose that is not merely unilateral but rather a combined purpose of both. This is the inevitable path that I must follow as a human being. 

Then, where is the point where my body and heart can occupy a unified position and move in one direction, drawing a straight line? To solve this problem, countless individuals and significant figures throughout history have lived and sacrificed, yet because we have not yet found a complete solution, humanity continues to groan.

Will there come a day when humanity can take pride in having a purpose, an inevitable purpose, that they can claim as their own before the universe or before God? We feel that this is a fateful and significant issue that humanity must resolve. Just as the ancients sought that unified purpose, we are also struggling to find it today.

When we consider whether any sage in the past drew a line… a "straight line" refers to the line drawn between two points, but we know that there has been no sage who has provided a point of purpose that can be drawn straight like this. While there may be paths leading toward that direction, no one has definitively stated, "This is the direction; it must be aligned with this." Furthermore, we know that no one throughout the historical ages has established a more valuable path that I must pursue.

In light of this, the place humanity must seek is not a place that has already been reached. It is a place that must be reached; therefore, it is not the present place. It is a place that must be sought in the future, and only in the future can the true self, the unified path where the true self can reside, appear. Thus, humanity has forgotten the present and has sought the future, which we understand very well as the historical direction.

In the present, such a path cannot be sought. That path will only appear in the future, beyond today. The completion of a single point in the future is an inevitable fact; therefore, if there are those who desire to reach such a standard, or those who wish to transcend human ethics and seek heavenly ethics, they will always strive toward that place, dedicating their lives to it, or revering it. We know that such a path has been the path of religion.

The goal pursued by religion, nations, and ideologies
In guiding the path of religion… the path of religion does not urge those who are present to fulfill their mission at that time; rather, it denies the time they are staying in to push them toward a better tomorrow. This direction has remained until now, and we know that this path will continue to be a pioneering path from now on.

We know that there are prophets in the history of religion. In every era, prophets have emerged to represent that era, prophesying that we must follow the conclusion where the direction can align with the future purpose, bringing humanity closer to the goals they desire. 

These prophets come to announce that we should not remain in that era. They say we should not stay in that time but rather stay in the future. Before Jesus came, John the Baptist appeared and said, "Repent, for the kingdom of heaven has come." He did not say, "Repent, for the kingdom of heaven is here." Jesus also came to this earth as a prince or as a Messiah carrying the mission of building the kingdom of heaven, yet he did not say that the kingdom of heaven had come. He stood in the same position as John the Baptist, saying, "Repent, for the kingdom of heaven is near." Because the kingdom of heaven is near, it indicates that the day when the kingdom of heaven can come is approaching; it does not claim that the kingdom of heaven is already here.

In this light, the three years of public life that Jesus led with his disciples were not a life within the kingdom of heaven. It was undoubtedly a life directed toward the kingdom of heaven. Jesus bore the cross not in the kingdom of heaven but in the position directed toward the kingdom of heaven. Furthermore, when Jesus said he would return, he did not say it from a position where he was already present; he said it from a position where he was not yet present.

Considering this, what kind of place did Jesus desire for the kingdom of heaven? Is that place one that has already appeared in the course of human history, or is it a place that is currently manifest, or is it a place that can appear in the future? That place is neither a currently manifest place nor one that has already appeared. It is a place that can appear in the future, which he introduced. Therefore, the mission of Christianity is not limited to this era; it is a mission to inherit the future.

From this perspective, many religions today, excluding Christianity, are the same. Among all the religions that have existed until now, has there been a religion that has reached the endpoint of the purpose humanity desires and claimed, "You must come here to live. You can only live by coming here"? There has been none. Religion undoubtedly sketches a victorious future toward tomorrow, toward a certain inevitable endpoint, while committing to a gradual process.

When we say that religion is leading the ideological or internal aspect, we must consider the historical path that the cultural sphere centered around religious thought and the people practicing religion must tread. The era in which humanity lives cannot be a time that aligns with the aspirations of those within that historical realm. It must be a process of preparation that transcends and resolves that era, moving toward the future.

On this earth, there are countless human beings. There are numerous nations. There are many religions. There are many ideologies. Nevertheless, we know that the ultimate goal pursued by nations, religions, and ideologies is undoubtedly to envision a unified world as humanity, to reach a place where they can take pride in their existence as victorious beings before the universe.

The inevitable destination
So, which religion is ahead in pursuing that ultimate purpose? Which religion is leading the way? There must be such a religion. Furthermore, which nation is at the forefront, running toward that ideal world, toward a unified purpose? There must be such a nation. Also, when we ask which ideology is leading the world, there must be an ideology that stands at the forefront of the world. However, these three must not be separated into their own distinct positions. Religions must converge at a single conclusion with nations, and nations must find a common destination that can be said to be the inevitable purpose centered around ideologies. Only then will the mission of religion conclude. There, the historical mission that humanity has sought will also conclude, and the unified world pursued by ideologies will be realized.

Therefore, it cannot be merely any religion centered around religion, nor can it be any single national ideology centered around patriotism. It cannot be any unilateral ideology centered around democracy or communism. The ideology must represent the entirety of human life. It must be an ideology that can represent the body and the heart, and it must be an ideology that I can hope for. The ideology I can hope for must be one that our family cannot help but desire to reach, and it must be the ultimate ideology that the nation can aspire to. It must be the overall standard that the country and the world can claim, "This is ours. This is what we have hoped for. This is the path to victory."

Only there will unification unfold; it cannot be merely religion as religion, or any specific nation as a nation. It cannot be merely an ideology as an ideology. Within that ideology, there must be nations, and within religions, there must be nations as well. There must be something that can encompass all three, allowing them to become one. This is the conclusion that we must reach without finding a point of unity.

Only by transcending that can we see the unified ideology that I can hope for, centered around myself, from a higher dimension that humanity has pursued throughout the historical era. Without transcending that position, we cannot surpass the dawn of the historical era that has come before. We cannot hope for a new morning of new hopes, nor can we welcome the rising sun of a new world that is being established. It is needless to say that such a time will come, and in the end, we can conclude that what one loves, what one cherishes, what one advocates, and what one fights for with their life cannot be the condition for grace.

Those who believe in a religion must transcend that religion; they must possess something else that can firmly negate and surpass their own beliefs, or they will inevitably remain in a sorrowful, incomplete position as losers. Similarly, if it is a nation, one cannot simply center on the nation they love and declare, "This is a one-way street!" It is impossible to reach that world without possessing a new national ideology that transcends the national thought and can leap beyond all traditional patriotic thoughts.

The same goes for ideological claims. Whether it is communism or democracy, one cannot simply follow that one ideology. Why? Because the body and heart are in conflict, and one cannot follow any unilateral aspect. The body commands the heart, and the heart commands the body, always operating from a conflicting standpoint. We know too well that because they are in a position of separation, they cannot avoid the path of struggle throughout life.

The end must focus on the future and be organized

Paul said that the law of the heart and the law of the body are in conflict with each other. "Oh, wretched man that I am! Who will deliver me from this body of death?" he lamented. Even Paul felt this. What about Jesus? Jesus also fought with a clear mind in that struggle. Jesus was a person too. However, centered on God's love, he was in a position where both body and heart could submit, emphasizing God's will over his own.

In other words, it may seem that a wife who only serves her husband has disappeared, but she will inevitably conquer him without fighting. Is that right or not? Even if the husband does not command or educate his wife, when the husband wants to care for her until the end, the wife will want to care for him even if told not to. This principle must be found.

Why did the body and heart fight? It is because the "I" has emerged. What was the motivation for the archangel's fall? It was due to the self-awareness of "I." The fall began from that self-awareness. A woman who retains self-awareness will not be able to become one with her husband even if she gets married. One must acknowledge the subjectivity of the subject.

Therefore, for fallen humanity to be saved, one must negate their self-awareness and establish a subjectivity centered on God. Because I am a relative being, I must negate my relative awareness and establish a subjective awareness, and from there, a new restoration movement of humanity begins. It can develop a new heart (心田). No matter how you look at it, it is like that.

What is a dutiful child? It exists solely for the parents. It does not exist for itself. What is a loyal subject? It exists only for the king. What is a virtuous woman? She exists only for her husband. Isn't that right? From there, the ideal unfolds. In a position where one can give, in a position where one can receive...

Then what position does God hold? Until now, God has not worked for Himself from a subjective position, but has worked for the sake of the other. That is why He is God, and that is why He is the subject. He is always the subject. To serve that subject as the subject, what must I do? To become an absolute counterpart, absolute obedience is required. This is the absolute low-pressure system and the secret to absolute unity. Isn't that so?

When a wife asks her husband, "Do you truly love me?" and he replies, "Oh, I love you. I love you more than the world. But..." it means he does not want to. When he says, "But there is still this much left in my heart," would that feel good? This means he is centered around himself. When he says, "There is still this much left," what was once good now feels unpleasant. The same goes for this. Therefore, be absolutely present. Live absolutely for each other. A man was not born for another man, nor was a woman born for another woman. They were born for each other. A woman was born for a man. A woman was not born for another woman, and a man was not born for another man.

From this perspective, all beings do not exist for themselves, but for each other. They act for each other. We cannot help but reach this conclusion.

The inevitable path of destiny that humanity must take - the path of love
So, in today's global end times, when looking at one's own religion, if one is in a position that does not align with the direction God is heading, asserting oneself in that position will lead to ruin. If a nation does not align with God's providential history, it will perish. If any ideology does not align with that, it will also perish.

What is the secret to not perishing? There must be a movement of thought that can only serve the subject from a position that can overcome everything. Therefore, one must understand God's circumstances, know God's hopes, and understand God's heart, and only then can one rise to that level. To become a virtuous woman before her husband, one must understand the husband's circumstances, desires, and heart. Only from there will a new religious perspective, a new national perspective, and a new worldview manifest.

The manifested, unified content of that connection is something that any human being can demand, any citizen can demand, and anyone throughout the past, present, and future of human history can demand. What is the subject? It is love. Therefore, one must be encompassed by a world that can only serve that love and be able to praise the value of one's life in a position united with the whole subject to reach a more absolute ideal type. Only then can one enter into the innermost room where God resides. Only the path of love is like that. No matter how much a worker's daughter, no matter how ignorant, or how uneducated she may be, if she establishes a love relationship with the sovereign of that nation, she can become the queen of that nation. It is the same principle. Today, fallen humanity may be in a miserable position, only able to become a sacrifice for Satan, but if they establish a love connection with God, they can not only enter into the heavenly palace but also freely come and go.

Because of this, humanity can reach the highest hope they desire, and knowing this, God has introduced His love to humanity. This is the inevitable path of destiny that humanity must take, the inevitable conclusion, and the inevitable course of history. Therefore, one must find the self that can be centered on this, find the family, find the nation, and find the world. Only by being able to host God can one finally reach the conclusion of the original self, a unified self where body and heart are not divided.

By doing so, humanity can settle the history of humanity and can confidently appear as God's son, holding the cosmic value of having triumphed as a human being. This is the path of the highest desire of humanity, and it is a path that humanity must inevitably pursue.

<Prayer> This year, we have spent from January to August under the tremendous title of "Protecting the Unification Front." Today is the third day of September, and it is the first Sabbath of this month. 

This morning, I spoke on the topic of "The Inevitable Path." To reach the place you desire and can love, you must become the embodiment of the love of your unified body and heart. However, because you have fallen and cannot be in such a position, you have become a servant of Satan and a member of the lineage of death.

The path of salvation to revive this is religion, and within that religious thought, the history of Christianity remains as a way to cover the ideology of the bride and bridegroom. Therefore, I believe that the Christian cultural sphere, representing the democratic world in the emotional aspect centered on this subjective thought, has inevitably emerged in a leading position.

In this world, democracy that can only love one's own country has already reached the end of its experiment. It is a tragic fact that it has not become a democracy that sacrifices one's own country to pursue a broader world for the sake of the heavenly subject, even if it means sacrificing one's own country to save the world.

Father, today we have come to know this, and we have launched a movement to break free from the nationalism that is trapped in the patriotism centered on one nation. Therefore, we have taught that one must transcend their own tribe. One must not love their own bloodline more than their nation.
You should not love your own race more than humanity. You should not love God less than humanity.

The direction toward unification has already been presented. The world of purpose has already been presented. I have now realized that the only inevitable path of destiny is to restore the essence of rest centered on the emotional life of our Father, following the hope that our Father desires through the circumstances of our Father in this place. Therefore, I must take pride in the love of our Father being in my heart. I must recognize that our Father is connected to me.

If I go east, then the parents can also go east because of the connection between parents and children. As the son of our Father, I know that the Father, as a parent, cannot help but follow wherever the son goes. I also know that we cannot help but follow where our Father is. Although our positions may differ, we know that the place we are bound is one. The place we want to meet is also centered on mutual love, and I have come to understand that only our Father’s love is our happiness and that only our Father’s love is the path of our lives.

We have fought to look forward to this, so we must fight until the end. We must fight to the very last. No matter how strong the enemy may be, I have realized that I cannot have the subjectivity to encompass this with the power of love without facing it directly. Therefore, I must quietly pray in the secret place for that path and follow the way of love, knowing that this is the way of heaven. We must go beyond the path of death. I have understood that if we do not follow this path, even if it means abandoning our country, the country will perish. I have come to know that we have a mission to awaken humanity by standing at the forefront for the manifestation of a new humanity, even if it means abandoning the humanity of the past. This vast responsibility is what the group of unification carries. Without abandoning the individual, we cannot find the family; without abandoning the family, we cannot find the race our Father desires; without abandoning the race, we cannot find the nation our Father desires; and without abandoning the nation on this earth, we cannot inherit the world our Father desires. Therefore, we have set out to forsake everything.

Our wish is solely for unification centered on our Father. My individual self must unify body and mind centered on our Father, and so must the family, the church, and the nation. Even when looking at the divided Korean entity, we are in a position where we must do so. There is no other way than to bind both sides, right and left, centered on our Father himself, so that ten fingers can be tied together as one. We hope that our Father will become the center of a new ideological nation in this country.

This world is also divided left and right, and the key point that can solve this is Korea. We know that by discerning this in Korea, it can ignite a global fire, and we are fighting with this understanding. In the midst of looking forward to the destiny of unification, we ask, Father, to help us with the conflicting positions of the North and South. Please bless us to seek a new path where we can feel our Father’s personality and God’s worldview through our Father’s love, and guide us in this endeavor.

We have come to understand that without becoming a people who desire the transcendent, unification cannot be achieved. Therefore, we must fight for this path. We must pioneer this path. We cannot tolerate evil for this path. We must focus solely on good, and we must become heavenly warriors who can march boldly with the flag of victory while not getting tired on the path of struggle, facing the final enemy. I earnestly ask that we may become sons and daughters loved by our Father.

Thus, we will inherit the path you have come to and will surely follow it. We will fight and follow until we fulfill the nation you have come to. We will surely follow until we fulfill the world you have come to. I swear at this moment to follow you even to the point of death to your place of love, so please accept this.

I have come to know that this is the inevitable path humanity must take centered on our Father’s love. Through the circumstances of our Father and along with God’s wishes, may I become a son who can stimulate our Father’s heart and be loved, and a son who can love our Father. May I pursue the vast path of desires to become a couple that our Father can love and rise to the position of parents that our Father can love. I earnestly ask that you help us not to become dropouts on this path, carrying the hope of hopes, becoming builders of tomorrow, leaving something for tomorrow, embracing tomorrow, and living for tomorrow, for this is the group of unification. I earnestly request that you make this realization anew at this time, and I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.
